Has T*log but missing T*epsilon, T, and standalone log. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 17:** Has T*c0 but no T*epsilon or T*log. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 18:** `T*c0*epsilon*exp(c1*epsilon) + T*c2*exp(c3*epsilon) + T*c4 + c5*epsilon + c6 + c7*epsilon**(1/5) + c8*epsilon*exp(c1*epsilon)`
If c1=0, c3=0: `T*c0*epsilon + T*c2 + T*c4 + c5*epsilon + c6 + c7*epsilon^(1/5) + c8*epsilon`
This gives T*epsilon, T, epsilon, constant, epsilon^(1/5) — but no T*log or log. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 19:** No T*epsilon or T*log. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 20:** `T*c0 + T*c1*epsilon**c2 + c3*epsilon + c4*exp(c5*epsilon)*sin(c6*epsilon + c7) + c8*epsilon**2 + c9`
If c2=1: T, T*epsilon. Missing T*log. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 21:** `T*c0*epsilon**c1 + ...` No T*log. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 22:** `T*c0 + c1*epsilon + c2*exp(c3*epsilon)*sin(c4*epsilon + c5) + c6*cos(c7*log(T*c8 + c9*epsilon + 1))`
The cos(log(T*c8 + c9*epsilon + 1)) mixes T and epsilon inside cos(log(...)). This cannot produce T*epsilon + T*log(epsilon+1) terms. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 23:** sin terms, no T*epsilon or T*log. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 24:** sin terms, no T*epsilon or T*log. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 25:** `T**c0*c1*epsilon**c2 + ...` Could set c0=1 to get T*epsilon (c2=1), but no T*log. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 26:** No T dependence. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 27:** `T*c0*sin(c1*epsilon + c2) + T*c3 + c4*exp(c5*epsilon)/(c6 + epsilon) + c7*epsilon*exp(c5*epsilon)/(c6 + epsilon) + c8*epsilon/(c6 + epsilon)`
Has T*sin, T, and rational/exp terms. No T*epsilon or T*log. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 28:** No T dependence. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 29:** `T*c0*epsilon + T*c1*log(c2*epsilon**2 + 1) + c3*epsilon**2 + c4*exp(c5*epsilon) + c6*epsilon*log(T*c7 + 1) + c8`
Has T*epsilon, T*log(c2*epsilon²+1), epsilon², exp, epsilon*log(T*c7+1), constant.
GT needs T*log(epsilon+1), not T*log(epsilon²+1). These are different. Also epsilon*log(T+const) ≠ log(epsilon+1). **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 30:** `T*c0 + T*c1*epsilon**2 + c2*epsilon + c3*exp(c4*epsilon)*sin(c5*epsilon + c6) + c7*epsilon**2 + c8*epsilon*exp(c9*epsilon)`
No T*log. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 31:** No T*log. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 32:** No T dependence. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 33:** `T*c0 + T*c1*sin(c2*epsilon + c3) + c4*epsilon + c5*exp(c6*epsilon) + c7*log(T*c8 + c9*epsilon + 1)`
Has log(T*c8 + c9*epsilon + 1) which mixes T and epsilon. This cannot separate into T*log(epsilon+1) + log(epsilon+1). **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 34:** No T*log or T*epsilon (unless c0,c2 chosen). `T**c0*c1*epsilon**c2` with c0=1 gives T*epsilon. But no T*log. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 35:** `T*c0 + T*c1*sin(c2*epsilon + c3) + T**c4*c5*exp(c6*epsilon) + T**c4*c7 + c8*epsilon`
If c4=1: T, T*sin, T*exp, T, epsilon. No T*log. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 36:** No T dependence. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 37:** `c0*exp(c1*epsilon) + c2*epsilon*log(c3*epsilon + 1) + c4*sin(c5*log(T*c6 + c7*epsilon + 1) + c8)`
Has sin(log(T+epsilon+...)) mixing T and epsilon. Cannot produce T*epsilon or T*log separately. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 38:** sin terms, no T*epsilon or T*log. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 39:** `T*c0 + T*c1*sin(c2*epsilon + c3) + T*c4*epsilon*sin(c5*epsilon + c6) + c7*epsilon + c8*epsilon`
Has T*epsilon*sin — not the right basis. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 40:** `c0*epsilon**2 + c1*exp(c2*epsilon) + c3*sin(c4*log(T*c5 + c6*epsilon + 1) + c7) + c8*epsilon**c9`
sin(log(T+epsilon+...)) mixes variables. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 41:** No T dependence. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 42:** `T*c0*epsilon + T*c1 + c2*epsilon**2 + c3*exp(c4*epsilon) + c5*epsilon + c6*log(T*c7 + 1)*sin(c8*epsilon + c9)`
Has log(T)*sin(epsilon) — this mixes T and epsilon in a non-separable way that can't match T*log(epsilon+1). **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 43:** `c0*epsilon**2 + c1*exp(c2*epsilon) + c3*epsilon*log(T*c4 + 1) + c5*sin(c6*log(c7*epsilon + 1) + c8)`
Has epsilon*log(T+1) which gives T-dependence through log(T). GT has linear T dependence. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 44:** `c0*exp(c1*epsilon) + c2*epsilon*exp(T*c3) + c4*epsilon**2 + c5*sin(c6*log(c7*epsilon + 1) + c8)`
Has exp(T) — wrong basis. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 45:** sin(log(T+epsilon+...)) — mixes variables. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 46:** `T*c0 + T**c1*c2*sin(c3*epsilon + c4) + c5*epsilon + c6*exp(c7*sin(c8*epsilon + c9))`
No T*epsilon or T*log. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 47:** No T dependence. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 48:** `T*c0 + T*c1*sin(c2*epsilon + c3) + T*c4*sin(c5*epsilon + c6) + c7*epsilon + c8*exp(c9*epsilon)`
sin terms, no T*epsilon or T*log. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 49:** `T*c0*epsilon + T*c1*sin(c2*epsilon + c3) + c4*epsilon**2 + c5*exp(c6*epsilon) + c7*epsilon*log(T*c8 + 1) + c9`
Has epsilon*log(T+1) — not T*log(epsilon+1). **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 50:** `T*c0 + c1*epsilon**2 + c2*exp(c3*epsilon) + c4*epsilon*log(T*c5 + 1) + c6*sin(c7*log(c8*epsilon + 1) + c9)`
Has epsilon*log(T+1) — wrong structure. **NO MATCH**
